    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 9.99999997e-07);
    u_xlat0.x = log2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_36 + -2.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * 0.159154952;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = exp2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 50.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(abs(u_xlat16_2.x), 9.99999997e-07);
    u_xlat0.x = log2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = exp2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 50.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor2.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);

    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x + u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * (-u_xlat16_17.xxx) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat10_3 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_17.xyz, u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat10_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = log2(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_7.x = exp2(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xxx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(abs(u_xlat16_38), 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat30 = clamp(u_xlat30, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_17.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat30 * u_xlat30;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat31) + _SLDir.xyz;

    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 9.99999997e-07);
    u_xlat0.x = log2(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * 0.159154952;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = exp2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 50.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = exp2(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = 2.0 / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = dot((-u_xlat3.xyz), u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x + u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * (-u_xlat16_17.xxx) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat10_3 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_17.xyz, u_xlat16_7.x);

    u_xlat16_7.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = log2(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_7.x = exp2(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xxx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_7.xyz;

    u_xlat16_7.x = min(abs(u_xlat16_38), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = exp2(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.y * u_xlat16_9.z + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.z * u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat20.x = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.00999999978);
    u_xlat20.x = min(u_xlat20.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat20.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat20.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = textureLod(_MatMap, u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat16_7.x).xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _Color0.xyz * u_xlat16_9.yyy + u_xlat16_9.xxx;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _Color1.xyz * u_xlat16_9.zzz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _Color2.xyz * u_xlat16_9.www + u_xlat16_8.xyz;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_4.w + _MetallicOffsetCoin;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_9.y * _Metallic0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_9.x + u_xlat16_27;
    u_xlat16_36 = _Metallic1 * u_xlat16_9.z + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = _Metallic2 * u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_36;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_8.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_36;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32 = min(max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = 2.0 / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = dot((-u_xlat3.xyz), u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x + u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * (-u_xlat16_17.xxx) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);

#else

#endif
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_36;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(0.25, 0.25, 0.25);

    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat3.xyz), u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);

    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat1.xy * u_xlat0.xy + u_xlat20.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy + _MatMap_ST.zw;

    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_9.x + u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.y * u_xlat16_9.z + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.z * u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat20.x = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.00999999978);
    u_xlat20.x = min(u_xlat20.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat20.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat20.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat10_4.w + _MetallicOffsetCoin;

    u_xlat16_36 = _Metallic2 * u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_36;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_8.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = 2.0 / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;

{
    u_xlat0.xy = _MatMap_ST.xy + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

    u_xlat16_32 = min(max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;

{

    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.zw, 0.0, 1.0);

    vs_TEXCOORD1 = in_COLOR0;

    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);

    vs_TEXCOORD1 = in_COLOR0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_9.x + u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.y * u_xlat16_9.z + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.z * u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat20.x = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.00999999978);
    u_xlat20.x = min(u_xlat20.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat20.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat20.x;

    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_8.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32 = min(max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;

    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat30 = min(max(u_xlat30, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat30 = clamp(u_xlat30, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;

vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _poke_ST.xy + _poke_ST.zw;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = min(max(vs_TEXCOORD0.zw, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.zw, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = in_COLOR0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTexM;

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNR2;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;

float u_xlat30;
float u_xlat31;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = _MatMap_ST.xy + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xx * u_xlat0.xy + vec2(1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat20.xy = _Time.xx * _MatMapSpeed.xy;
    u_xlat20.xy = fract(u_xlat20.xy);
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[0].zxy + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat31 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat31 = max(u_xlat31, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat31);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat31) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * (-u_xlat3.yzx);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * (-u_xlat3.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * (-u_xlat3.zxy);
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat3.yzx) * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_BumpMapNR2, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.www + vec3(_RoughNessOffset0, _RoughNessOffset1, _RoughNessOffset2);
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_BumpMapNR, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_5.w + _RoughNessOffsetCoin;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz + (-u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MainTexM2, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_5.wwww + vec4(-0.0, -0.333333313, -0.666666687, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_9 * vec4(3.19148946, 3.19148946, 3.19148946, 3.19148946);
    u_xlat16_9 = -abs(u_xlat16_9) + vec4(1.03191495, 1.03191495, 1.03191495, 1.03191495);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_9 = min(max(u_xlat16_9, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_9 = clamp(u_xlat16_9, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_9.z + u_xlat16_9.y;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(0.25, 0.25, 0.25);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat3.xyz), u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat1.xy * u_xlat0.xy + u_xlat20.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy + _MatMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_9.y;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_9.x + u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.y * u_xlat16_9.z + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.z * u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat20.x = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.00999999978);
    u_xlat20.x = min(u_xlat20.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat20.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat20.x * u_xlat20.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = textureLod(_MatMap, u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat16_7.x).xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _Color0.xyz * u_xlat16_9.yyy + u_xlat16_9.xxx;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _Color1.xyz * u_xlat16_9.zzz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _Color2.xyz * u_xlat16_9.www + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTexM, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_4.w + _MetallicOffsetCoin;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_9.y * _Metallic0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_9.x + u_xlat16_27;
    u_xlat16_36 = _Metallic1 * u_xlat16_9.z + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = _Metallic2 * u_xlat16_9.w + u_xlat16_36;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_8.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32 = min(max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul) + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = 2.0 / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = dot((-u_xlat3.xyz), u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x + u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * (-u_xlat16_17.xxx) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_17.xyz, u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = log2(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_7.x = exp2(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xxx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(abs(u_xlat16_38), 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_38;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat30 = min(max(u_xlat30, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat30 = clamp(u_xlat30, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_17.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat30 * u_xlat30;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat31) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat31) + _SLDir.xyz;
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 9.99999997e-07);
    u_xlat0.x = log2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_36 + -2.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * 0.159154952;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = exp2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 50.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(abs(u_xlat16_2.x), 9.99999997e-07);
    u_xlat0.x = log2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = exp2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 50.0);

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor2.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;

 Pass {
  Name "ShadowCaster"
  LOD 300
  Tags { "IGNOREPROJECTOR" = "true" "LIGHTMODE" = "SHADOWCASTER" "QUEUE" = "Geometry" "RenderPipeline" = "LightweightPipeline" "RenderType" = "[_RenderType]" }
  Cull Off
  GpuProgramID 82434
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "gles " {
"// hash: 3b88408ef73e2427
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _BaseMap_ST;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowBias;
uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 100

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif
precision highp int;
#define SV_TARGET0 gl_FragData[0]
void main()
{
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
